<script type="text/javascript">

    var wizStartUpMethod = "1";
    function WizFloater() {
        var prom = (("https:" == document.location.protocol) ? "https://" : "http://");
        var domainUrl = "alljobs.wizsupport.com"; var profile = "3"; var subject = ""; var lang = "he"; var scriptname = "FloatingChat";
        script = document.createElement("script"); script.type = "text/javascript"; script.async = true; script.onload = function () { };
        wizSrc = prom + domainUrl + "/chat/" + scriptname + ".aspx?T=-1,,/SearchResultsGuest.aspx,NonMobile,3,-1,,&profile=" + profile + "&subject=" + subject;
        wizSrc += "&lang=" + lang + "&url=" + escape(window.location) + "&refer=" + escape(document.referrer) + "&title=" + escape(document.title);
        script.src = wizSrc;
        document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    };


    if (wizStartUpMethod == "2") { addEvent("DOMContentLoaded", document, function () { WizFloater() }, false); } else { setTimeout(WizFloater, 3000); }

    function addEvent(evnt, elem, func) {
        if (elem.addEventListener)  // W3C DOM
            elem.addEventListener(evnt, func, false);
        else if (elem.attachEvent) { // IE DOM
            if (evnt == "DOMContentLoaded") { evnt = "readystatechange"; }
            elem.attachEvent("on" + evnt, func);
        }
        else { // No much to do
            elem[evnt] = func;
        }
    }

</script>
